 isse pehle kohli ko isisi ke saal ke sarvshereshth van-de cricketer kaa puraskaar bhi mila tha
 Kohli said, i am happy to get this award in front of so many cricketers, whom i have seen playing and been inspired to see them
 ummid karata hum ki maujuuda satr main bhi main is pradarshan ko jari rakhuunga

 Tendulkar also thanked the BCCI for always supporting him, whether he was doing well or not or was injured

 Laxman said, When i was young, i wanted to play for India
 maine apana sapana puraa kiya
